                            Dataset
                        

                        
                            

                                Id
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        nyis-y4yr
                                    
                                
                            

                        
                            

                                Name
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        DOB Sign Application Filings
                                    
                                
                            

                        
                            

                                Attribution
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        Department of Buildings (DOB)
                                    
                                
                            

                        
                            

                                Attribution Link
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        http://www.nyc.gov/html/dob/html/codes_and_reference_materials/foilmonthly.shtml#sign
                                    
                                
                            

                        
                            

                                Description
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        A list of sign applications filed for a particular day and associated data. Prior monthly reports are archived at DOB and are not available on NYC Open Data.
                                    
                                
                            

                        
                            

                                Category
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        Housing & Development
                                    
                                
                            

                        
                            

                                Tags
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        [signs, dob, buildings]
                                    
                                
                            

                        
                            

                                Created
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        2013-04-18T15:18:57Z
                                    
                                
                            

                        
                            

                                Publication Date
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        2017-03-28T20:05:58Z
                                    
                                
                            

                        
                            

                                Rows Updated
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        2017-03-28T20:05:38Z
